, sans-serif; font-size: 16pt;\"><span style=\"color: #333333; font-size: 12pt;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-weight: normal;\">This text contains is a typical procedure used on one of my previous ships to convert from high brix (93) Columbian Molasses to MEG fibre grade for UCC.<o:p></o:p></span></span></span></b></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 13.5pt; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; margin-left: -6.0pt; margin-right: 25.45pt; margin-top: 0in; text-align: justify;\">\n<b style=\"mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , sans-serif; font-size: 16pt;\"><br />\n</span></b></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 13.5pt; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; margin-left: -6.0pt; margin-right: 25.45pt; margin-top: 0in; text-align: justify;\">\n<b style=\"mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , sans-serif; font-size: 16pt;\"><span style=\"color: #333333; font-size: 12pt;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-weight: normal;\">Olefins, Pthalates, Adipates, Fatty acids and Fatty alcohols are bad previous cargoes for next wall wash cargoes.<o:p></o:p></span></span></span></b></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 13.5pt; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; margin-left: -6.0pt; margin-right: 25.45pt; margin-top: 0in; text-align: justify;\">\n<b style=\"mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , sans-serif; font-size: 16pt;\"><br />\n</span></b></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 13.5pt; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; margin-left: -6.0pt; margin-right: 25.45pt; margin-top: 0in; text-align: justify;\">\n<b style=\"mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , sans-serif; font-size: 16pt;\"><span style=\"color: #333333; font-size: 12pt;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-weight: normal;\">Wall wash test for Mono Ethylene Glycol fibre grade is the most stringent.<o:p></o:p></span></span></span></b></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 13.5pt; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; margin-left: -6.0pt; margin-right: 25.45pt; margin-top: 0in; text-align: justify;\">\n<b style=\"mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , sans-serif; font-size: 16pt;\"><br />\n</span></b></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 13.5pt; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; margin-left: -6.0pt; margin-right: 25.45pt; margin-top: 0in; text-align: justify;\">\n<b style=\"mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , sans-serif; font-size: 16pt;\"><i><span style=\"color: blue; font-size: 12pt;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-weight: normal;\">When you take a wall wash ensure the tank is perfectly dry&nbsp;</span></span></i><span style=\"color: #333333; font-size: 12pt;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-weight: normal;\">( especially zinc coated tanks ). There can be no sea spray as WWT is a weather permitting procedure especially for MEG (fg) where chlorides fail for union carbide corporation&nbsp;at 0.249 ppm.&nbsp;Tell master to alter course during ventilation and wall wash.&nbsp;FW rinse&nbsp;area around tank entrance to remove salt from sticking to shoe cover. Suspect like a paranoid moron that every thing that the methanol comes in contact with ,&nbsp;till you write down the results could be dirty . Do not be stingy with lab methanol.&nbsp;Ensure your sweat drop does not alter results.<o:p></o:p></span></span></span></b></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 13.5pt; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; margin-left: -6.0pt; margin-right: 25.45pt; margin-top: 0in; text-align: justify;\">\n<b style=\"mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , sans-serif; font-size: 16pt;\"><br />\n</span></b></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 13.5pt; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; margin-left: -6.0pt; margin-right: 25.45pt; margin-top: 0in; text-align: justify;\">\n<b style=\"mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , sans-serif; font-size: 16pt;\"><i><span style=\"color: blue; font-size: 12pt;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-weight: normal;\">Wallwash is taken from 4 parts of all 4 bulkheads\u2014but not from corners</span></span></i><i><span style=\"color: #333333; font-size: 12pt;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-weight: normal;\">,</span></span></i><span style=\"color: #333333; font-size: 12pt;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-weight: normal;\">which do not count as a standard value. Surveyors must be accompanied inside tanks by a responsible person.<o:p></o:p></span></span></span></b></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 13.5pt; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; margin-left: -6.0pt; margin-right: 25.45pt; margin-top: 0in; text-align: justify;\">\n<b style=\"mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , sans-serif; font-size: 16pt;\"><br />\n</span></b></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 13.5pt; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; margin-left: -6.0pt; margin-right: 25.45pt; margin-top: 0in; text-align: justify;\">\n<b style=\"mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , sans-serif; font-size: 16pt;\"><span style=\"color: #333333; font-size: 12pt;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-weight: normal;\">For&nbsp;Wall&nbsp;Wash</span></span><span style=\"color: blue; font-size: 12pt;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-weight: normal;\">&nbsp;</span><i><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-weight: normal;\">take into the tank one litre of Methanol. Only 200 cc 1/5 of this amount is brought out for testing</span></i><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-weight: normal;\">.</span></span><span style=\"color: #333333; font-size: 12pt;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-weight: normal;\">&nbsp;After filling up squirt bottle with methanol, analyse for HC and CL first before taking into the tank.<o:p></o:p></span></span></span></b></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 13.5pt; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; margin-left: -6.0pt; margin-right: 25.45pt; margin-top: 0in; text-align: justify;\">\n<b style=\"mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , sans-serif; font-size: 16pt;\"><br />\n</span></b></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 13.5pt; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; margin-left: -6.0pt; margin-right: 25.45pt; margin-top: 0in; text-align: justify;\">\n<b style=\"mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , sans-serif; font-size: 16pt;\"><span style=\"color: #333333; font-size: 12pt;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-weight: normal;\">WWT surveyor must not wash more than 6 feet height. He also cannot wash the bottom unless you are loading&nbsp;Hexene 1/ potable Ethanol etc..&nbsp;Floor areas are tested by placing ( not wiping ) filter paper on a spot wetted by Methanol. This paper is placed inside a sample bottle and 50 cc test Methanol is added for every piece of filter paper. If any surveyor wipes bulkheads with Methanol soaked instead of squirting Methanol using a polyethylene squirter , tell the master as this is not a representative sample of the action of liquid on the bulkhead .<o:p></o:p></span></span></span></b></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 13.5pt; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; margin-left: -6.0pt; margin-right: 25.45pt; margin-top: 0in; text-align: justify;\">\n<b style=\"mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , sans-serif; font-size: 16pt;\"><br />\n</span></b></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 13.5pt; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; margin-left: -6.0pt; margin-right: 25.45pt; margin-top: 0in; text-align: justify;\">\n<b style=\"mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , sans-serif; font-size: 16pt;\"><span style=\"color: #333333; font-size: 12pt;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-weight: normal;\">Methanol spray by crew to beat the surveyor is not a bright deed in the context of MEG FG as all you do is to bring the dirt from sides to bottom. So mop bottom sides with sponges and DI water.&nbsp;No rags are allowed as more than 10 suspended particles in the first foot sample fails for MEG FG.&nbsp;Use torch beam at zero incidence in a dark tank to detect lint shed from paper shoe covers.<o:p></o:p></span></span></span></b></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 13.5pt; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; margin-left: -6.0pt; margin-right: 25.45pt; margin-top: 0in; text-align: justify;\">\n<b style=\"mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , sans-serif; font-size: 16pt;\"><br />\n</span></b></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 13.5pt; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; margin-left: -6.0pt; margin-right: 25.45pt; margin-top: 0in; text-align: justify;\">\n<b style=\"mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , sans-serif; font-size: 16pt;\"><span style=\"color: #333333; font-size: 12pt;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-weight: normal;\">Various tests done all over the world are---- (remember all of them may not be applicable to your cargo, so find out well in time.&nbsp;The main ones are HC, CL and PTT. )<o:p></o:p></span></span></span></b></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 13.5pt; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; margin-left: -6.0pt; margin-right: 25.45pt; margin-top: 0in; text-align: justify;\">\n<b style=\"mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , sans-serif; font-size: 16pt;\"><br />\n</span></b></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 13.5pt; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; margin-left: -6.0pt; margin-right: 25.45pt; margin-top: 0in; text-align: justify;\">\n<b style=\"mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , sans-serif; font-size: 16pt;\"><span style=\"color: #333333; font-size: 12pt;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-weight: normal;\">1)Visual first impression</span></span><span style=\"color: #333333; font-size: 12pt;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-weight: normal;\">.<o:p></o:p></span></span></span></b></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 13.5pt; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; margin-left: -6.0pt; margin-right: 25.45pt; margin-top: 0in; text-align: justify;\">\n<b style=\"mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , sans-serif; font-size: 16pt;\"><span style=\"color: #333333; font-size: 12pt;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-weight: normal;\">No condensation moisture on cold interface bulkheads or deck head,no blistered or open splits on epoxy coating, no white coloured patches of Zinc salts or Calcium and Magnesium sea water salts , no black rouge Fe3O4 tattoed into stainless steel active surfaces&nbsp;from oxidised welds, no red Fe(OH)3 due to boiler water alkaline additives etc, no green vitriol Ferrous Sulphate patched on stainless steel active areas.&nbsp;Use Bufferclean Citric acid of pH 5.5 to remove salts from zinc tanks and adsorbed ( this is a surface phenomenon in zinc tanks and is different from absorbed ) previous cargo reactant matter.&nbsp;Dye out is an organic stain remover.<o:p></o:p></span></span></span></b></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 13.5pt; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; margin-left: -6.0pt; margin-right: 25.45pt; margin-top: 0in; text-align: justify;\">\n<b style=\"mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , sans-serif; font-size: 16pt;\"><br />\n</span></b></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 13.5pt; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; margin-left: -6.0pt; margin-right: 25.45pt; margin-top: 0in; text-align: justify;\">\n<b style=\"mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , sans-serif; font-size: 16pt;\"><span style=\"color: #333333; font-size: 12pt;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-weight: normal;\">2)Odour of tank<o:p></o:p></span></span></span></b></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 13.5pt; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; margin-left: -6.0pt; margin-right: 25.45pt; margin-top: 0in; text-align: justify;\">\n<b style=\"mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , sans-serif; font-size: 16pt;\"><span style=\"color: #333333; font-size: 12pt;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-weight: normal;\">Meg is odour absorbing . Use lac to remove odour in SS tanks. Acrylates have their own smell killers like Monoethanolamine and air fresheners marketed by tankcleaning chemical companies. After a strong smell cargo if the next cargo is odor sensitive the seals of tank dome / butterworth ports may have to be exchanged. Pyridine cargoes give very strong odour.<o:p></o:p></span></span></span></b></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 13.5pt; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; margin-left: -6.0pt; margin-right: 25.45pt; margin-top: 0in; text-align: justify;\">\n<b style=\"mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , sans-serif; font-size: 16pt;\"><br />\n</span></b></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 13.5pt; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; margin-left: -6.0pt; margin-right: 25.45pt; margin-top: 0in; text-align: justify;\">\n<b style=\"mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , sans-serif; font-size: 16pt;\"><span style=\"color: #333333; font-size: 12pt;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-weight: normal;\">3)</span></span><span style=\"color: red; font-size: 12pt;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-weight: normal;\">Colour&nbsp;</span></span><span style=\"color: #333333; font-size: 12pt;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-weight: normal;\">of Methanol wash</span></span><span style=\"color: #333333; font-size: 12pt;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-weight: normal;\"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></b></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 13.5pt; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; margin-left: -6.0pt; margin-right: 25.45pt; margin-top: 0in; text-align: justify;\">\n<b style=\"mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , sans-serif; font-size: 16pt;\"><span style=\"color: #333333; font-size: 12pt;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-weight: normal;\">Colour&nbsp;5 Apha&nbsp;(or Saybolt ASTM D12095)&nbsp;is required for the MEG fg wash&nbsp;( highest spec.) .</span></span><i><span style=\"color: blue; font-size: 12pt;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-weight: normal;\">&nbsp;Must see in day light or fluorescent light against a white sheet of paper at night.&nbsp;Use the magnifying glass or even your reading glasses<o:p></o:p></span></span></i></span></b></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 13.5pt; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; margin-left: -6.0pt; margin-right: 25.45pt; margin-top: 0in; text-align: justify;\">\n<b style=\"mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , sans-serif; font-size: 16pt;\"><br />\n</span></b></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 13.5pt; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; margin-left: -6.0pt; margin-right: 25.45pt; margin-top: 0in; text-align: justify;\">\n<b style=\"mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , sans-serif; font-size: 16pt;\"><span style=\"color: #333333; font-size: 12pt;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-weight: normal;\">Apha solution is platinum chloride solution. The number of cc Apha solution ( min is 5 cc ) for Apha 5 added to distilled water gives the shade number.<o:p></o:p></span></span></span></b></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 13.5pt; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; margin-left: -6.0pt; margin-right: 25.45pt; margin-top: 0in; text-align: justify;\">\n<b style=\"mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , sans-serif; font-size: 16pt;\"><br />\n</span></b></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 13.5pt; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; margin-left: -6.0pt; margin-right: 25.45pt; margin-top: 0in; text-align: justify;\">\n<b style=\"mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , sans-serif; font-size: 16pt;\"><span style=\"color: #333333; font-size: 12pt;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-weight: normal;\">Lightest is +30 Saybolt and darkest is -16 used only in the petroleum industry.&nbsp;Water White standard colour is in the range of&nbsp;+30 to +20.<o:p></o:p></span></span></span></b></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 13.5pt; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; margin-left: -6.0pt; margin-right: 25.45pt; margin-top: 0in; text-align: justify;\">\n<b style=\"mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , sans-serif; font-size: 16pt;\"><br />\n</span></b></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 13.5pt; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; margin-left: -6.0pt; margin-right: 25.45pt; margin-top: 0in; text-align: justify;\">\n<b style=\"mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , sans-serif; font-size: 16pt;\"><span style=\"color: #333333; font-size: 12pt;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-weight: normal;\">Apha zero means clear. In your wall wash lab you must have comparator nessler tube ready made solutions of A5&nbsp;A10&nbsp;and A20 ( always in multiples of 5 ).<o:p></o:p></span></span></span></b></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 13.5pt; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; margin-left: -6.0pt; margin-right: 25.45pt; margin-top: 0in; text-align: justify;\">\n<b style=\"mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , sans-serif; font-size: 16pt;\"><br />\n</span></b></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 13.5pt; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; margin-left: -6.0pt; margin-right: 25.45pt; margin-top: 0in; text-align: justify;\">\n<b style=\"mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , sans-serif; font-size: 16pt;\"><span style=\"color: #333333; font-size: 12pt;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-weight: normal;\">The standard apha solutions are stable for many days but should be done again after one week. The stock solution is stable for an indefinite period if kept in a refrigerator.<o:p></o:p></span></span></span></b></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 13.5pt; margin-bottom: .0001pt; Extreme of pH can interfere with test. Check every 5 minutes . PTT test detects all inhibited chemicals.&nbsp;Make new KMNO4 solution every 3 days and store in an amber coloured bottle.Under purest condition PTT test will run for 120 minutes. PTT test fails only when contaminants react with KMNO4. HC does not react with KMNO4.&nbsp;So PTT time can be increased by Bleach or Chlorinated solvents . , sans-serif; font-size: 16pt;\"><br />\n</span></b></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; margin-left: -6.0pt; margin-right: 25.45pt; margin-top: 0in; text-align: justify;\">\n<b style=\"mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , sans-serif; font-size: 16pt;\"><span style=\"color: #333333; font-size: 12pt;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-weight: normal;\">The Potassium permanganate solution should be stored in brown bottles and in the dark.<o:p></o:p></span></span></span></b></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; margin-left: -6.0pt; margin-right: 25.45pt; margin-top: 0in; text-align: justify;\">\n<b style=\"mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , sans-serif; font-size: 16pt;\"><span style=\"color: #333333; font-size: 12pt;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-weight: normal;\">Even if the PTT test taken on board before arrival passed, gives no quarantee to have the same result from the surveyors test. (Different spots taken by surveyor).<o:p></o:p></span></span></span></b></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; margin-left: -6.0pt; margin-right: 25.45pt; margin-top: 0in; text-align: justify;\">\n<b style=\"mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , sans-serif; font-size: 16pt;\"><br />\n</span></b></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 13.5pt; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; margin-left: -6.0pt; margin-right: 25.45pt; margin-top: 0in; text-align: justify;\">\n<b style=\"mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , sans-serif; font-size: 16pt;\"><span style=\"color: #333333; font-size: 12pt;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-weight: normal;\">Glass apparatus that have a `brown film' should not be used as it is Manganese di-oxide, the reduced product of potassium permanganate. This will catalyse the oxidation/reduction decolorisation process of potassium permanganate and will give less PTT time. Glassware is cleaned by overnight immersion in an acid bath of 50% hydrochloric acid. The clean tubes must then rinsed well in tap water followed by DI water / Methanol.<o:p></o:p></span></span></span></b></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 13.5pt; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; margin-left: -6.0pt; margin-right: 25.45pt; margin-top: 0in; text-align: justify;\">\n<b style=\"mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , sans-serif; font-size: 16pt;\"><br />\n</span></b></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 13.5pt; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; margin-left: -6.0pt; margin-right: 25.45pt; margin-top: 0in; text-align: justify;\">\n<b style=\"mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , sans-serif; font-size: 16pt;\"><span style=\"color: #333333; font-size: 12pt;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-weight: normal;\">Similarly, the flask&nbsp;containing stock solution of potassium permanganate requires cleaning between batches of fresh solution. The last rinse should be with fresh potassium permanganate solution and not methanol.<o:p></o:p></span></span></span></b></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 13.5pt; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; margin-left: -6.0pt; margin-right: 25.45pt; margin-top: 0in; text-align: justify;\">\n<b style=\"mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , sans-serif; font-size: 16pt;\"><span style=\"color: #333333; font-size: 12pt;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-weight: normal;\">Glass apparatus that have a `brown film' should not be used as it is Manganese di-oxide, the reduced product of potassium permanganate. This will catalyse the oxidation/reduction decolorisation process of potassium permanganate and will give less PTT time. Glassware is cleaned by overnight immersion in an acid bath of 50% hydrochloric acid. The clean tubes must then rinsed well in tap water followed by DI water / Methanol.<o:p></o:p></span></span></span></b></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 13.5pt; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; margin-left: -6.0pt; margin-right: 25.45pt; margin-top: 0in; text-align: justify;\">\n<b style=\"mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , sans-serif; font-size: 16pt;\"><span style=\"color: #333333; font-size: 12pt;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-weight: normal;\">Similarly, the flask&nbsp;containing stock solution of potassium permanganate requires cleaning between batches of fresh solution. This substance must not come into contact with the skin and NEVER be pipetted by mouth. Treat the Uranyl nitrate/ Cobaltous chloride standard solution with care.<o:p></o:p></span></span></span></b></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 13.5pt; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; margin-left: -6.0pt; margin-right: 25.45pt; margin-top: 0in;\">\n<b style=\"mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , sans-serif; font-size: 16pt;\"><br />\n</span></b></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 13.5pt; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; margin-left: -6.0pt; margin-right: 25.45pt; margin-top: 0in; text-align: justify;\">\n<b style=\"mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , sans-serif; font-size: 16pt;\"><span style=\"color: #333333; font-size: 12pt;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-weight: normal;\">8)NVM :<o:p></o:p></span></span></span></b></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 13.5pt; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; margin-left: -6.0pt; margin-right: 25.45pt; margin-top: 0in; text-align: justify;\">\n<b style=\"mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , sans-serif; font-size: 16pt;\"><span style=\"color: #333333; font-size: 12pt;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-weight: normal;\">To determine the weight of residue left on the surface. Spray Acetone / Hexane on a small area. If sprayed area has a visible boundary ( bur n marks ), non volatile matter is there.&nbsp;NVM consists of high BP sediments, dirt, rust etc.<o:p></o:p></span></span></span></b></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 13.5pt; , sans-serif; font-size: 16pt;\"><span style=\"color: #333333; font-size: 12pt;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-weight: normal;\">Ashore it is done by evaporating the Methanol wash and weighing.<o:p></o:p></span></span></span></b></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 13.5pt; , sans-serif; font-size: 16pt;\"><i><span style=\"color: blue; font-size: 12pt;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-weight: normal;\">Go to tank and collect 200cc of wash in a clear bottle. To achieve this you must&nbsp;squirt at least 500 cc from a polyethylene squirter to allow for spillage. Never miss the leading edge of dirty wash flowing down the wall</span></span></i><span style=\"color: #333333; font-size: 12pt;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-weight: normal;\">.&nbsp;Make your own funnel by slicing off a Polyethelene bottle with an extremely sharp box cutter blade.&nbsp;Mate it on a porthole glass pour methanol and see it does not spill even a drop. The neck of this funnel must lead direct into the sample bottle ( narrow neck ). With a gloved hand you must be able to hold both, the other hand for the squirter.When you dispose wash Methanol in CCR sink run the water tap as a safety measure lest it gasses up a sleeping seaman in a cabin.<o:p></o:p></span></span></span></b></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 13.5pt; , sans-serif; font-size: 16pt;\"><span style=\"color: #333333; font-size: 12pt;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-weight: normal;\">The method of not involving Nitric acid in the Chloride test could pass a ship staff tank WWT ,&nbsp;while a shore gas ion chromatograph will fail the sample for Mono Ethylene Glycol fibre grade.&nbsp;Nitric acid decomposes Sodium Cyanide and Sodium Sulphide which otherwise form precipitate with AgNO3 and thus interfere with the lab test.<o:p></o:p></span></span></span></b></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 13.5pt; LEST YOU  RUE AT LEISURE LATER.</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot;;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , sans-serif;\">THE <st1:place st=\"on\"><st1:placename st=\"on\">AMAZON</st1:placename> <st1:placetype st=\"on\">RIVER</st1:placetype></st1:place> IS 4000 MILES LONG JUST A HUNDRED MILES SHORTER THAN <st1:place st=\"on\">NILE</st1:place> --THE WORDS LONGEST RIVER.  BUT IT MORE THAN MAKES UP BY ITS SHEER STRENGTH AND VOLUME--- AMAZON POURS 2000 TIMES MORE WATER THAN THE <st1:place st=\"on\">NILE</st1:place> .  ONE BY FIFTH OF THE FRESH WATER THE  WORLDS OCEANS RECEIVE IS FROM THE AMAZON.  </span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , sans-serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , sans-serif;\">IT FLOWS EASTWARDS FROM THE SNOW CAPPED <st1:place st=\"on\">ANDES</st1:place> INTO THE <st1:place st=\"on\">NORTH ALTANTIC</st1:place> AND IS NAVIGABLE ALMOST ITS ENTIRE LENGTH.  IT DEPOSITS APPROX 70 TONS OF SEDIMENT EVERY MINUTE AT ITS DELTA WHICH IS 100 MILES WIDE AND LESS SALINE 200 MILES INTO THE OCEAN.  SMALL SIZE SHIPS REACH <st1:city st=\"on\"><st1:place st=\"on\">IQUITOS</st1:place></st1:city> IN <st1:country-region st=\"on\"><st1:place st=\"on\">PERU</st1:place></st1:country-region> 2300 MILES UPRIVER. LARGE OCEAN LINERS REACH <st1:city st=\"on\"><st1:place st=\"on\">MANAUS</st1:place></st1:city>  1000 MILES UPSTREAM.   </span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , sans-serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , sans-serif;\">THE TIDAL INFLUENCE IS FELT AS FAR AS OBIDOS. MOST OF THESE PIRANHAS ARE VEGETARIANS UNLESS YOU WANT TO OFFER A BLOODY FINGER.   </span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , sans-serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , sans-serif;\">WHEN  THE RIVER IS FLOODED  THE CREST IS 50 FEET ABOVE <st1:city st=\"on\"><st1:place st=\"on\">NORMAL</st1:place></st1:city> ,  THE SPRING  EBB TIDES IN RAINY SEASON  NOV TO JUNE ARE 6 KNOTS WITH HUGE UPROOTED TREES FLOATING DOWN WHOM YOU MUST DODGE.  IF CAUGHT ON THE BOWS IT REDUCES SHIPS SPEED ,  IF YOUR PROPELLER HITS A TREE TRUNK  YOU CAN HAVE A PROBLEM.  </span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , sans-serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , sans-serif;\">WHEN THE  COASTAL FEATURES ARE SUBMERGED  LAND CANNOT  NOT BE RECOGNISED EASILY.  TALL GRASS WHICH GROWS OUT OF WATER CAN ADD TO THE CONFUSION.  THE GPS IS THE BEST BET.  THE WGS 84 CORRECTION IS NEGLIGIBLE.   DURING FLOODS ALL THE SNAKES MIGRATE TO HIGH GROUND AND IF YOU LIKE TO  GET BITTEN BY SNAKES WHO ARE SHORT OF PATIENCE THIS IS THE PLACE TO BE AT. </span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , sans-serif;\"><br /></span>\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"https://1.bp.blogspot.com/-vGm2NyjmN80/XHQN6-y8cgI/AAAAAAABf8E/e0yAIpyFRv4ytV-RwXjXOTblK3Vco1o7wCLcBGAs/s1600/dodddwnload.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" data-original-height=\"146\" data-original-width=\"346\" height=\"270\" src=\"https://1.bp.blogspot.com/-vGm2NyjmN80/XHQN6-y8cgI/AAAAAAABf8E/e0yAIpyFRv4ytV-RwXjXOTblK3Vco1o7wCLcBGAs/s640/dodddwnload.jpg\" width=\"640\" /></a></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , sans-serif;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , sans-serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , sans-serif;\">SOMETIMES IN SEPT OR MARCH YOU CAN SEE THE POROROCA OR THE SPECTACULAR TIDAL BORE LIKE WE HAVE IN THE HOOGHLY RIVER\u2014ONLY DIFFERENCE IS THIS ONE IS ABOUT 5 METRES HIGH AND ITS CREST IS WHITE FOAM AS IT FORCES ITS WAY 400 MILES UPSTREAM AT 40 KNOTS.  IT CAN BE UNNERVING IF YOU DO NOT UNDERSTAND WHAT IT IS. </span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , sans-serif;\"><br /></span>\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<iframe allowfullscreen=\"\" class=\"YOUTUBE-iframe-video\" data-thumbnail-src=\"https://i.ytimg.com/vi/CyZCFyuR_Sk/0.jpg\" frameborder=\"0\" height=\"266\" src=\"https://www.youtube.com/embed/CyZCFyuR_Sk?feature=player_embedded\" width=\"320\"></iframe></div>\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<br /></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , sans-serif; font-size: 9pt;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , sans-serif;\">ALL TYPES ON INSECTS INVADE YOUR SHIP.  SOME OF THEM ARE GOOD IN SELF DEFENCE.  FOR EXAMPLE THERE IS A LARGE COCKROACH ABOUT 4 INCHES LONG WHICH IF YOU TRY TO TRAMPLE WILL SEND A SHARP QUILL THROUGH YOUR SAFETY SHOE SOLE INTO YOUR LEG.&nbsp;</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , sans-serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , sans-serif; font-size: small;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\">AND THERE IS THIS WORLD RECORD HOLDING 18 INCH HERMAPHRODITIC LEECH WITH A 6 INCH HYPODERMIC NEEDLE. &nbsp;IMAGINE IT CAN HOLD 3 TIMES ITS OWN WEIGHT IN ONE FEEDING. IT BREATHES THROUGH ITS SKIN. AND ITS SALIVA CONTAINS ANTICOAGULANTS WHICH CAN BLEED YOU TO DEATH.</span></span><br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TO00VlR9kGI/AAAAAAAAAsU/7h0Bt7-I8z8/s1600/images+%25285%2529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"267\" src=\"https://3.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TO00VlR9kGI/AAAAAAAAAsU/7h0Bt7-I8z8/s400/images+%25285%2529.jpg\" width=\"400\" /></a></div>\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , sans-serif; font-size: small;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-size: 12px;\"><br />\n</span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , sans-serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , sans-serif;\"> SOME BEETLES ARE ALLERGY CAUSING AND CAN SLAM SHUT YOUR EPIGLOTIS.  I REMEMBER ONCE SAVING MY MATE\u2019S LIFE WITH AN INSTANT  SHOT OF CHLOR PHENERAMINE MALEATE INJECTION.  BETTER TO HAVE ANTI MALARIA TABLETS.  KEEP YOUR ACCOMODATION AND EVEN CARGO TANKS SHUT.   </span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , sans-serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , sans-serif;\">CLOUDS OF FIREFLIES AT NIGHT CAN BE SUCH A WONDERFUL SIGHT.  OR DOZENS OF GREEN PARROTS DURING DAY.   LIGHTNING IN THE SKY  LOOKS LIKE ARTILLERY FIRE. </span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , sans-serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , sans-serif;\">AT <st1:city st=\"on\"><st1:place st=\"on\">MANAUS</st1:place></st1:city>  <st1:place st=\"on\">RIO NEGRO</st1:place> HAS ITS CONFLUENCE WITH AMAZON AND STAINS IT WITH BLACK INKY ORGANIC MATTER.   MALARIA , TYPHOID, HEPATITIS AND CHOLERA GERMS ARE WAITING TO TAKE YOU ON  IN THIS NECK OF THE WOODS.</span><br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TO0z8EEd9fI/AAAAAAAAAsM/DS3mp3DrWGk/s1600/images+%25281%2529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; text-align: center;\">\n<br /></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , sans-serif; font-size: 9pt;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , sans-serif; font-size: 9pt;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , sans-serif; font-size: 9pt;\"><o:p> </o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TO02RFRzr3I/AAAAAAAAAsY/bEka0XLclso/s1600/images+%25287%2529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"640\" src=\"https://3.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TO02RFRzr3I/AAAAAAAAAsY/bEka0XLclso/s640/images+%25287%2529.jpg\" width=\"426\" /></a></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , sans-serif; font-size: 9pt;\"><o:p><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-weight: bold;\"><br />\n</span></o:p></span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , sans-serif;\"><o:p> <span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-weight: bold;\"><span style=\"font-size: 9pt;\">B</span>USINESS:</span></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , sans-serif;\"><o:p><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-weight: bold;\"><br />\n</span></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , sans-serif;\">ENOUGH OF LORE.  LETS GET TO BUSINESS.  CROSS BARRANORTE OR THE NORTH BAR AT HIGH WATER ON A RISING TIDE.  THE BOTTOM HERE IS SOFT MUD. BE CAREFUL IF THE SHIP IS POUNDING DUE TO SWELL IN WHICH CASE ALLOWANCES FOR UKC HAS TO BE MADE.&nbsp;</span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , sans-serif;\"><br /></span>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , sans-serif;\">&nbsp;THE TIDE SETS HERE IN A SW/ NE DIRECTION. FROM THE BA ADMIRALTY TIDE TABLE CALCULATIONS FOR SECONDARY PORT BARRANORTE YOU MUST SUBTRACT 2HRS 36 MIN FOR HW AND 3HRS 20 MIN FOR LW. THE DEEPEST PART OF BAR  HAS SHIFTED TO 4 MILES  SOUTHWARDS OF THE LIGHT SHIP . IT TAKES 2 HOURS TO CROSS THE BAR. </span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , sans-serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , sans-serif;\">AFTER CROSSING THE BAR INWARDS YOU REACH A BOTTLENECK CALLED CURUA CHANNEL.  SUBTRACT ONE HOUR FROM BARRANORTE BA ATT TIMES TO GET CURUA CHANNEL TIDAL TIMES.  THE BUOYS THERE ARE OUT OF POSITION MOST OF THE TIME.&nbsp;</span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , sans-serif;\"><br /></span>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , sans-serif;\">SO BEFORE ARRIVAL ASK THE AGENTS TO SEND YOU THE LATEST BUOY POSITION.  IN THIS L ( <st1:city st=\"on\"><st1:place st=\"on\">LIMA</st1:place></st1:city> SHAPED <st1:city st=\"on\"><st1:place st=\"on\">BEND</st1:place></st1:city> ) KEEP TO THE GREEN BUOY SIDE OFF BUOYS 6 8 AND 10 AT 25 TO 75 RATIO.  THIS IS BECAUSE THE RED BUOY SIDE IS GETTING SILTED EASTWARD INTO THE CHANNEL . THE RED BUOYS 5 7 AND 9 CAN BE TRUSTED AS THEY ARE DEEP ANCHORED IN SILT AND CANNOT BE KNOCKED OVER.  </span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , sans-serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , sans-serif;\">THE THUMB RULE IS KEEP TO THE OUTER SIDE OF RIVER BENDS WHICH ARE  ARE SCOURED DEEPER. THE SAME IS THE CASE WITH CURUA CHANNEL. </span><br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-iUeyyirpcg4/TpqCMshSDJI/AAAAAAAAHBI/onHUvYrc3EU/s1600/imagesCAT3V0D4.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"299\" src=\"https://2.bp.blogspot.com/-iUeyyirpcg4/TpqCMshSDJI/AAAAAAAAHBI/onHUvYrc3EU/s400/imagesCAT3V0D4.jpg\" width=\"400\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , sans-serif;\">YOU MUST KNOW WHICH SIDE THE CURRENT/ WIND  WILL SET YOU.  DO NOT ATTEMPT TO PASS ANOTHER SHIP AT CURUA CHANNEL.  HERE IT IS ONE SHIP AT A TIME AS THERE IS NO SEA ROOM AT THE L BEND,  THE ACTUAL USABLE CHANNEL BEING ONLY 2,5 CABLES WIDE.  THE BUOYS ARE ONE MILE APART.   YOU CAN TRUST GPS POSITIONS IN THE CURUA CHANNEL.  TREE TRUNKS AND WEED CLUMPS AT NIGHT CAN DISORIENT YOU ON RADAR. </span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , sans-serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , sans-serif;\">AGENT CAN ALSO FAX YOU THE LOCAL TIDE TABLE PAGES .  THE PASSAGE FROM BARRA NORTE TO FAZENDINHA OR MACAPA PILOT STATION IS NON COMPULSORY PILOTAGE.  IF YOU WANT A PILOT BECAUSE YOU DO NOT HAVE  PROPER CHARTS YOU CAN EMBARK A PILOT AT SALINOUPOULIS OR ESPADARTE PILOT STATIONS WHICH IS 170 MILES FROM BARRA NORTE.&nbsp;</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , sans-serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , sans-serif;\">THE PILOTS IN THE AMAZON CAN BE TRUSTED. THEY VERY RARELY LOOK AT THE CHART.  THEY USE RADAR VRM MARKER TO SET CLEARING DISTANCES.  FROM MACAPA ONWARDS IT IS COMPULSORY PILOTAGE UPRIVER.  SHIP HAS TO ANCHOR AT MACAPA TO CLEAR THE PORT AUTHORITIES.  THE HARBOUR MASTER ALSO HAS A VISIT.  IF YOU HAVE ANY DAMAGE ON YOUR BOWS HE WILL HOLD A PROPER ENQUIRY. </span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-FkvUQGNIGMo/TpqB92jfLfI/AAAAAAAAHBA/PFQyDn7sPcA/s1600/imagesCAQZINS3.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"271\" src=\"https://3.bp.blogspot.com/-FkvUQGNIGMo/TpqB92jfLfI/AAAAAAAAHBA/PFQyDn7sPcA/s400/imagesCAQZINS3.jpg\" width=\"400\" /></a></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , sans-serif; font-size: 9pt;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , sans-serif; font-size: 9pt;\"><br /></span>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , sans-serif;\">AT MACAPA WHEN DROPPING OUTWARD PILOT WITH TIDE FROM BEHIND , FULLY LOADED , LITTLE SEAROOM AND SMALL CRAFT AROUND---- BE CAREFUL.   IF YOU HAVE TO WAIT , STEM THE TIDE SO THAT YOU CAN ANCHOR IF REQD .  AFTER MACAPA INBOUND EVEN THE LARGE SCALE BRAZILIAN  CHARTS ARE OF NO USE.  ON PASSAGE FROM MACAPA TO ITACOATIARA TWICE WE FOUND OUR SHIP NAVIGATING <st1:place st=\"on\"><st1:placename st=\"on\">HALF</st1:placename> <st1:placename st=\"on\">MILE</st1:placename> <st1:placename st=\"on\">DEEP</st1:placename> <st1:placename st=\"on\">INSIDE</st1:placename>  <st1:placetype st=\"on\">LAND</st1:placetype></st1:place> .&nbsp;</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , sans-serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , sans-serif;\">WHEN  YOU WANT TO PASS ANOTHER SHIP IN THE RIVER BETTER CLARIFY ON VHF IN ADVANCE IF IT IS GOING TO BE RED TO RED OR GREEN TO GREEN.</span><br />\n<br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , sans-serif;\">WHEN YOU FINALLY COME OUT OF THE RIVER, AND HEAD INTO THE ATLANTIC OCEAN&nbsp;WILL BE A BIT TAKEN ABACK BY THE&nbsp; LIMITED UKC INDICATED BY THE ECHOSOUNDER MACHINE , AND CLEAR CUM DISCOLOURED WATER SWIRLS ALONG THE SHIP SIDE. &nbsp;</span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , sans-serif;\"><br /></span>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , sans-serif;\">NOTHING TO WORRY ABOUT, AS THIS HUGE MASS OF MUDDY WATER ORGINATES FROM THE SUBTERRANEAN UNDERWATER AMAZON RIVER .&nbsp; THIS IS WHY THE WATER SALINITY IS VERY LOW AT THE MOUTH OF THE AMAZON,&nbsp; EVEN IF YOUR SHIP IS TWO HUNDRED MILES AWAY INTO THE ALTANTIC OCEAN , WITHOUT SOLITON WAVE FORMATION-- MUCH AGAINST THE PROPERTIES OF WATER&nbsp;. </span><br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-GdOxVRw8P9A/TpqBNJp8ZSI/AAAAAAAAHA4/3VeqpiwMnhg/s1600/amazon-delta-lg.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"640\" src=\"https://4.bp.blogspot.com/-GdOxVRw8P9A/TpqBNJp8ZSI/AAAAAAAAHA4/3VeqpiwMnhg/s640/amazon-delta-lg.jpg\" width=\"640\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , sans-serif;\">( IN BLACK SEA TOO THERE IS AN UNDERWATER STREAM FLOWING INTO BLACK SEA, WHILE THE SURFACE CURRENT IS OUTWARDS.)</span><br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<br /></div>\n<br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , sans-serif;\">KEEP THE <st1:place st=\"on\"><st1:placename st=\"on\">ENGINE</st1:placename> <st1:placetype st=\"on\">ROOM</st1:placetype> <st1:placetype st=\"on\">SEA</st1:placetype></st1:place> SUCTIONS ON HIGH. THIS WAY YOU CAN REDUCE SQUAT WHEN REQUIRED.</span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , sans-serif;\"><br /></span>\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"https://3.bp.blogspot.com/-XlLcH81weas/XHQNBKTi56I/AAAAAAABf7w/htVkLnLqmjooiFV0Idij4mpIlFHJ_LeGACLcBGAs/s1600/imwwwages.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" data-original-height=\"168\" data-original-width=\"300\" height=\"358\" src=\"https://3.bp.blogspot.com/-XlLcH81weas/XHQNBKTi56I/AAAAAAABf7w/htVkLnLqmjooiFV0Idij4mpIlFHJ_LeGACLcBGAs/s640/imwwwages.jpg\" width=\"640\" /></a></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , sans-serif;\"><br /></span>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , sans-serif;\"><br /></span>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , sans-serif;\"><br /></span>\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"https://1.bp.blogspot.com/-2DHRKZ2JD9g/XHQNQYdmoBI/AAAAAAABf74/zQwHGkTl8UALkwz0G18zYgberLW5uGmiQCLcBGAs/s1600/idffmages.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" data-original-height=\"169\" data-original-width=\"298\" height=\"362\" src=\"https://1.bp.blogspot.com/-2DHRKZ2JD9g/XHQNQYdmoBI/AAAAAAABf74/zQwHGkTl8UALkwz0G18zYgberLW5uGmiQCLcBGAs/s640/idffmages.jpg\" width=\"640\" /></a></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , sans-serif;\"><br /></span>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<span style=\"background-color: #f3f3f3; font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 24px;\">Capt. Ajit Vadakayil</a></cite><span class=\"icon user blog-author\" style=\"background-image: url(&quot;data:image/png; background-repeat: no-repeat; display: inline-block; font-weight: bold; height: 18px; margin: 0px 0px -4px 6px; width: 18px;\"></span><span class=\"datetime secondary-text\" style=\"margin-left: 6px;\"><a href=\"https://ajitvadakayil.blogspot.com/2019/02/sanatana-dharma-hinduism-exhumed-and_23.html?showComment=1551111310968#c3686331311549833835\" rel=\"nofollow\" style=\"color: #888888; text-decoration-line: none;\">February 25, 2019 at 9:45 PM</a></span></div>\n<div class=\"comment-content\" style=\"margin-bottom: 8px; text-align: justify;\">\n<span style=\"color: red;\">http://ajitvadakayil.blogspot.com/2016/01/point-break-movie-review-capt-ajit.html</span><br /><br />EXTRACT FROM POST ABOVE--<br /><br />QUOTE: One of my readers asked me to give one more example of an incident where I showed HUMAN SPIRIT at sea by breaking \u201clong established rules\u201d<br /><br />Well!-- OK, a WEE one !!!<br /><br />There was this time , my ship was coming out of a narrow tributary of mighty river Amazon. We were timed to cross a shallow bar at high water.<br /><br />While we were crossing the bar , I got a frantic call from Chief Engineer\u2014all temperatures of sea water cooled machinery ( main engines/ generators etc ) were rising rapidly \u2013with the added information that we are on HIGH sea suction which is nearly 4 metres above the ship\u2019s bottom LOW sea suction.<br /><br />This meant that river mud had ingressed the seawater inlet pipes.<br /><br />Chief Engineer arbitrarily informed that he wants to shut down the main engines and generators--lest the pistons get seized in the cylinders .<br /><br />I firmly commanded him\u2014\u201c You cannot stop any machinery till I order you to do it . Go to manual override . This is an emergency and I now control the ship\u2019s response \u201c<br /><br />Immediately I told the Brazilian river pilot\u2014I now have taken over your pilotage under Master\u2019s authority.<br /><br />I quickly consulted the chart and literally power waded the ship to a deep sliver of water. Meanwhile I had the anchors ready.<br /><br />As soon as I dropped anchor, I raced to the engine room. The ENTIRE engineers were there white faced with all sorts of alarms beeping.<br /><br />I quickly got the ship\u2019s fresh water tank hooked on to the generators using the \u201cinternational shore coupling\u201d and fire hose after knocking off a flange . The best part was that only I knew the pipelines\u2014I traced it then and there .<br /><br />The cooling water starved generators gasped back to life.<br /><br />I got the LOW sea suction opened up and got clean river water into the cooling systems.<br /><br />To cut a long story short we now had the mud cleared out and main engines and generators all running smooth.<br /><br />When I went back to the bridge the pilot said that we cant do night navigation in the tributary as per rules.<br /><br />I told him, we cant remain there for daylight as at the next turn of tide , the ships rudder would hit the river bank and then my brand new ship is history.<br /><br />I told him\u2014\u201cI WILL TAKE THE SHIP OUT IN DARKNESS . I KNOW THE RIVER BENDS , THE DEEPS AND SILTED AREAS . I WILL COMMIT IN WRITING\u201d<br /><br />Anyways , I got search lights out at the forecastle and we started our trip in absolute darkness with river bank trees almost brushing the ship at certain areas.<br /><br />The entire river tribals had taken out fire torches are were whistling and clapping as we whooshed past at terrific speed beating the fall of tide depth.<br /><br />Finally , as we exited the tributary and entered the mighty Amazon, the young pilot remarked that he was confident that I would do it. But if we had run aground , polluted and blocked the tributary, we both would have been in a Brazilian jail.<br /><br />The rest of my stunned crew could only say \u201c CAPTAIN DELIVERED AGAINST ALL ODDS-- AS USUAL \u201c.<br /><br />The grapevine had spread the engine crew has spread the world of how captain TOOK OVER TECHNICAL OPERATIONAL COMMAND OF THE ENGINE ROOM and how every order was followed without demur ..<br /><br />What I have said above is a tour de force.<br /><br />CONTINUED TO 2-</div>\n</div>\n<div class=\"comment-replies\" style=\"margin-left: 36px; margin-top: 1em;\">\n<div class=\"comment-thread inline-thread\" id=\"c3686331311549833835-rt\" style=\"background-color: #eeeeee; margin: 8px 0px; padding: 0.5em 1em;\">\n<ol class=\"thread-chrome thread-expanded\" id=\"c3686331311549833835-ra\" style=\"list-style-type: none; padding: 0px;\">\n<li class=\"comment\" id=\"c42795022270256247\" style=\"border-bottom: 0px; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 16px 0px 0px;\"><div class=\"avatar-image-container\" style=\"float: left; margin: 0.2em 0px 0px; max-height: 36px; overflow: hidden; width: 36px;\">\n</div>\n<div class=\"comment-block\" style=\"margin-left: 48px; position: relative;\">\n<div class=\"comment-header\" style=\"margin: 0px 0px 8px;\">\n<cite class=\"user\" style=\"font-style: normal; font-weight: bold;\"><a href=\"https://www.blogger.com/profile/14410812789424637654\" rel=\"nofollow\" style=\"color: #888888; text-decoration-line: none;\">Capt. There are major similarities with ancient Vedic practices.</div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\nFast is broken on Sankranti and Vinayaka Chaturthi only after sighting the moon at dawn.  The crescent moon rises 50 minutes after sun rise after new moon.  </div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\nThe crescent moon is on the forehead of Siva.  The flag of Islam has it. In Tamil Nadu the ancient Kabaaliswaran temple is a Shiva temple.<br />\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<object class=\"BLOGGER-youtube-video\" classid=\"clsid:D27CDB6E-AE6D-11cf-96B8-444553540000\" codebase=\"http://download.macromedia.com/pub/shockwave/cabs/flash/swflash.cab#version=6,0,40,0\" data-thumbnail-src=\"http://3.gvt0.com/vi/-G5U8T649Bc/0.jpg\" height=\"266\" width=\"320\"><param name=\"movie\" value=\"http://www.youtube.com/v/-G5U8T649Bc&fs=1&source=uds\" /><param name=\"bgcolor\" value=\"#FFFFFF\" /><embed width=\"320\" height=\"266\"  src=\"http://www.youtube.com/v/-G5U8T649Bc&fs=1&source=uds\" type=\"application/x-shockwave-flash\"></embed></object></div>\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\nWhere there is Siva there must be pure Ganga ( pure Zam Zam in the middle of a Mecca desert ).</div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\nSiva Lingam is a heavy black meteorite stone, from outer space , with mysterious powers and metaphysical energy to raise the Kundalini  .  A true lingam is so powerful that water has to drip on it to keep it in control.<br />\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-3DV6yBLf5qI/TqW2KPgS8_I/AAAAAAAAHSg/a-mfA-PmGZU/s1600/images%252B%252812%2529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://2.bp.blogspot.com/-3DV6yBLf5qI/TqW2KPgS8_I/AAAAAAAAHSg/a-mfA-PmGZU/s1600/images%252B%252812%2529.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\nThe black stone in the SE corner of the granite structure at Mecca called Al Hajar Ul Aswad 30 cms in diameter, 5 feet above the ground .<br />\n<br />\nIt is the south eastern corner stone of Kaaba. &nbsp; Here it is mirrored . &nbsp;The auspicious end in Hinduism vaastu is the \"Kanni moola\" or NW corner.<br />\n<br />\nIn all temples Hindus face west while praying as the diety doors face east.<br />\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\nThere were inscriptions in Sanskrit on the Kaaba stone.<br />\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<object class=\"BLOGGER-youtube-video\" classid=\"clsid:D27CDB6E-AE6D-11cf-96B8-444553540000\" codebase=\"http://download.macromedia.com/pub/shockwave/cabs/flash/swflash.cab#version=6,0,40,0\" data-thumbnail-src=\"http://0.gvt0.com/vi/O7Hzri0LyEw/0.jpg\" height=\"266\" width=\"320\"><param name=\"movie\" value=\"http://www.youtube.com/v/O7Hzri0LyEw&fs=1&source=uds\" /><param name=\"bgcolor\" value=\"#FFFFFF\" /><embed width=\"320\" height=\"266\"  src=\"http://www.youtube.com/v/O7Hzri0LyEw&fs=1&source=uds\" type=\"application/x-shockwave-flash\"></embed></object></div>\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\nVedic practices require devotees to enter temples in seamless white sheets.</div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\nVedic pradikshanam ( circumambulation )  is walking round 7 times, clockwise.   Muslims cannot kiss the black stone which activate the 7 chakras of the human body any more, emulating the kiss it received from the prophet, as the stone was broken in the middle ages and is now held by silver clamps and nails .  Devotees now point  to it at eack of the 7 counter clockwise circuits around the stone. </div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\nThe mysterious number 786 is sacred in Koran.  Nobody has been able to explain what it is, though it is printed on all Arabic Korans.<br />\n<br />\nWrite OM symbol ( sound frequency 7.83 Hertz ) in Sanskrit and keep it facing a mirror  and you can see like MAGIC  the number 786 in Devanagri script.</div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\nKaaba was a pilgrimage site for centuries, more from from the days on King Vikramaditya\u2014 even Guru Nanak ( a non muslim ) had been there .</div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\nEncyclopedia Britannica says Kaaba has 360 idols including a King Vikramaditya inscripted gold dish, in a temple chamber called <em>Ishalayam</em>. &nbsp;King Vikramaditya ruled 7500 years before the birth of Islam.&nbsp;Idol worship is banned in Islam.</div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\nIndian muslims must read above words with an open mind. After all the ancient Vedic culture or way of life belongs to every Indian and the sub-continenent --NOT just Hindus. &nbsp;Vedic culture existed 9500 years before the birth of Islam.<br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"background-color: yellow;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"background-color: yellow;\">Saraswati civilisation at the banks of river Saraswati from 9000 BC to 4000 BC &nbsp;is the cradle of world civilisation </span>. Saraswati river dried up in 4000 BC due to tectonic shift blocking the Himalayan glacier source, causing an exodus of elite to Mesopotamia, Europe, Russia and all over India. Indus valley civilisation started after the Saraswati river dried up, and Yamuna started pouring into Ganges.<br />\n<br />\nOne of my Pakistani Second Engineers, who had done religious studies in Khandahar and in Iran for many years , told me that every time he went to Mecca his friends and relatives would gives him dozens of silk handkerchiefs , to rub on the black stone . And every time he spent some time hurriedly doing that , he would get whipped quite severely by someone who was paid to do this (to time usurpers ) </div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<o:p> </o:p></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<o:p>&nbsp;  </o:p><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span class=\"apple-style-span\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot;;\"><span style=\"background: rgb(238 , 238 , 204); color: #333333;\">Ibn Battuta accounts say that Calicut King Cheman Perumal had a head priest cum accounts in-charge at the Shiva Temple ( called PAGAN temple by the west ) at Mecca which was a watering oasis for the camels , enroute to Jerusalem and Petra.&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span></span><span style=\"background: rgb(238 , 238 , 204); color: #333333; font-family: &quot;trebuchet ms&quot; , &quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 10pt; line-height: 115%;\"><br />\n<br />\n</span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot;;\"><span class=\"apple-style-span\"><span style=\"background: rgb(238 , 238 , 204); color: #333333;\">For whatever reasons, the disturbed King decided to make a trip to Mecca , as soon as he heard that Mohammed founded Islam and installed a black stone , on the SE corner of the Kaaba.&nbsp; </span></span></span><br />\n<br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot;;\"><span class=\"apple-style-span\">He took a ship from Calicut to Salalah and form there went by caravan route to Mecca. He met Mohammed , and the Islamic grapevine says that he was impressed by Islam and got converted from Hindu to Muslim.&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span class=\"apple-converted-space\"><span style=\"background: rgb(238 , 238 , 204); color: #333333;\">&nbsp;<o:p></o:p></span></span></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot;;\"><span class=\"apple-style-span\"><span style=\"background: rgb(238 , 238 , 204); color: #333333;\">The King\u2019s court at Calicut does NOT record this conversion, though messages were sent fast by carrier pigeons and hawks.</span></span><span class=\"apple-converted-space\"><span style=\"background: rgb(238 , 238 , 204); color: #333333;\">&nbsp;</span></span><span class=\"apple-style-span\"><span style=\"background: rgb(238 , 238 , 204); color: #333333;\">The Encyclopedia Islamia admits as much when it says: \"Muhammed's grandfather and uncles were hereditary priests of the Kaaba temple which housed 360 Vedic idols!\" The encyclopedia Britannica records ths too.&nbsp; </span></span></span><br />\n<br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot;;\"><span class=\"apple-style-span\">Ibn Battuta tells that Cheraman Perumal gave some tangy Calicut ginger pickle to Muhammed who ate it with great relish. The Prophet distributed it among his companions too. I also received a piece to eat --Hakim reports in 'Al Musthadrak</span>. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span class=\"apple-style-span\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot;;\"><span style=\"background: rgb(238 , 238 , 204); color: #333333;\">On the way back to Calicut, the king fell ill and was buried at Salalah, Oman ( some at Salalah say that he was killed ).. font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 18.4px;\">QUOTE: Al-Biruni wrote an encyclopedic work on India called \u201cTarikh Al-Hind\u201d (History of India) in which he explored nearly every aspect of Indian life, including religion, history, geography, geology, science, and mathematics. My book is nothing but a simple historic record of facts. I shall place before the reader the theories of the Hindus exactly as they are, and I shall mention in connection with them similar theories of the Greeks in order to show the relationship existing between them.(1910, Vol. 1, p. 7;1958, p. 5)<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"background-color: white; font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 18.4px;\">Hindus considered Muslims violent and impure, and did not want to share anything with him.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"background-color: white; font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 18.4px;\">Over time, Al-Biruni won the welcome of Hindu scholars. Al-Biruni collected books and studied with these Hindu scholars to become fluent in Sanskrit, discover and translate into Arabic the mathematics, science, medicine, astronomy and other fields of arts as practiced in 11th century India. He was inspired by the arguments offered by Indian scholars who believed earth must be ellipsoid shape, with yet to be discovered continent at earth's south pole, and earth's rotation around the sun is the only way to fully explain the difference in daylight hours by latitude, seasons and earth's relative positions with moon and stars.[36] Al-Biruni was also critical of Indian scribes who he believed carelessly corrupted Indian documents while making copies of older documents.[37] Al-Biruni's translations as well as his own original contributions reached Europe in 12th and 13th century, where they were actively sought.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"background-color: white; font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 18.4px;\">CONTINUED TO 2--<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"background-color: white; font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 18.4px;\">CONTINUED FROM 1--<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"background-color: white; font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 18.4px;\">While others were killing each other over religious differences, Al-Biruni had a remarkable ability to engage Hindus in peaceful dialogue. Mohammad Yasin puts this dramatically when he says, \u201cThe Indica is like a magic island of quiet, impartial research in the midst of a world of clashing swords, burning towns, and burned temples.\u201d (Indica is another name for Al-Biruni\u2019s history of India). Al-Khw\u0101rizm\u012b accomplished most of his work in the period between 813 and 833. After the Muslim conquest of Persia, Baghdad became the centre of scientific studies and trade, and many merchants and scientists from as far as China and India traveled to this city, as did al-Khw\u0101rizm\u012b. He worked in Baghdad as a scholar at the House of Wisdom established by Caliph al-Ma\u2019m\u016bn, where he studied the sciences and mathematics, which included the translation of Greek and Sanskrit scientific manuscripts.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"background-color: white; font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 18.4px;\">Al-Khw\u0101rizm\u012b's Z\u012bj al-Sindhind[11] (Arabic: \u0632\u064a\u062c \u0627\u0644\u0633\u0646\u062f \u0647\u0646\u062f\u200e, \"astronomical tables of Sindh and Hind\") is a work consisting of approximately 37 chapters on calendrical and astronomical calculations and 116 tables with calendrical, astronomical and astrological data, as well as a table of sine values. This is the first of many Arabic Zijes based on the Indian astronomical methods known as the sindhind.[22] The work contains tables for the movements of the sun, the moon and the five planets known at the time. This work marked the turning point in Islamic astronomy. Hitherto, Muslim astronomers had adopted a primarily research approach to the field, translating works of others and learning already discovered knowledge.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"background-color: white; /></a></div>\n<br />\n<br />\nTHE MEANING OF REAL WORK</div>\n<div>\n<br /></div>\n<div>\nthe owner of the favourite restaurant of a big city went for a surprise visit.</div>\n<div>\n<br /></div>\n<div>\nfor the past 6 months the hotel had CHANGED FROM A HUGE PROFIT MAKING </div>\n<div>\nMACHINE TO A LOSS MAKING UNIT--he wanted to check out why- personally.</div>\n<div>\n<br /></div>\n<div>\nthe staff and cooks were the same--- the only change was the new sprightly </div>\n<div>\nmanager of the restaurant--who joined 6 months back.</div>\n<div>\n<br /></div>\n<div>\nthe owner asked the manager --how is my hotel doing?-- </div>\n<div>\n<br /></div>\n<div>\nmanager says ,we have been accredited iso 49000 since i joined-- we have </div>\n<div>\n4.99 marks in HMSA ( that is something like our own TMSA ) -- i have </div>\n<div>\nstreamlined the paperwork-- here are the pie charts--here are the trends </div>\n<div>\nin colour-- here are the consumptions and the averages-- we have </div>\n<div>\ncentralised our accounts and purchases and economised on vegetables and</div>\n<div>\nmeats --here are the figures --this is the last inspection report of the municipality </div>\n<div>\n--we scored 100%-- blah blah --he was on his own trip--</div>\n<div>\n<br /></div>\n<div>\nthe owner got upset ,walked off and called the stewards--in private. </div>\n<div>\nwhat do you think is the problem? why have all our regular customers </div>\n<div>\ndeserted us? why are the chairs empty?.</div>\n<div>\n<br /></div>\n<div>\nthe stewards said--lot of them sat for half an hour and before cooks </div>\n<div>\ncould get the soup ready --they got up in  a huff and cursed us and went </div>\n<div>\naway. we are also resigning--we too don't like to stand here the whole </div>\n<div>\nday picking our noses , waiting for the cows to come home --we are losing</div>\n<div>\nout on tips--</div>\n<div>\n<br /></div>\n<div>\nthen the owner went into the kitchen-- and found the cooks caught in THE </div>\n<div>\nCHAKRAVYUH OF ACTIVITY TRAPS doing tabulations on A4 size papers , </div>\n<div>\naverages, inventories , cleaning, pressure testing pipes, stencilling , </div>\n<div>\npolishing pans and buttons of their tunics, testing fuel  -- the whole </div>\n<div>\nkitchen smelled of strong metal cleaner/ detergent instead of food-- </div>\n<div>\n<br /></div>\n<div>\nhe asked the chief cook who was walking past him in a tearing hurry-- </div>\n<div>\n<br /></div>\n<div>\n----are you coming or going? </div>\n<div>\n<br /></div>\n<div>\n--the man says -WHAAA?</div>\n<div>\n<br /></div>\n<div>\n<br /></div>\n<div>\nEXTREME EXAMPLE OF ACTIVITY TRAP-- A CHIEF ENGINEER OF A SHIP WHO HAS BRAINWASHED HIMSELF THAT--  THE PURPOSE OF HIS SHIP IS TO TAKE HIS MAIN ENGINES FROM POINT A TO POINT B.</div>\n<div>\n<br /></div>\n<div>\nhow many of you have lost the plot and are caught in the chakravyuh of daily activity traps? style=\"font-style: normal; font-weight: bold;\"><a href=\"https://www.blogger.com/profile/14410812789424637654\" rel=\"nofollow\" style=\"color: #888888; text-decoration-line: none;\">Capt. Ajit Vadakayil</a></cite><span class=\"icon user blog-author\" style=\"background-image: url(&quot;data:image/png; background-repeat: no-repeat; display: inline-block; font-weight: bold; height: 18px; margin: 0px 0px -4px 6px; width: 18px;\"></span><span class=\"datetime secondary-text\" style=\"margin-left: 6px;\"><a href=\"https://ajitvadakayil.blogspot.com/2009/07/real-work-and-activity-traps-capt-ajit.html?showComment=1512359197169#c7121907320141828550\" rel=\"nofollow\" style=\"color: #888888; text-decoration-line: none;\">December 4, 2017 at 9:16 AM</a></span></div>\n<div class=\"comment-content\" id=\"bc_0_21MC\" style=\"margin-bottom: 8px; text-align: justify;\">\nSOMEBODY ASKED ME TO ELABORATE A BIT MORE ON ACTIVITY TRAP<br /><br />ON MY SHIP I DO NOT ALLOW PARASITES TO THRIVE.<br /><br /><br />EVER SEEN A HAMSTER RUNNING UP AND WHEEL WHICH GOES ROUND AND ROUND . THERE ARE MANY SUCH HUMAN HAMSTERS OCCUPYING CHAIRS OF OFFICE MANAGERS<br /><br />The activity trap is the risk of becoming so busy with an activity as to forget what it is supposed to achieve. You lose sight of your goalpost. You climb up a ladder only to find out it is leaning against the wrong wall. It is the risk of becoming so busy with activity so as to forget and miss the aim of that activity<br /><br />The activity trap is the \u201ctyranny of the mundane.\u201d It includes the trivial issues, red tape, requests, and routine meaningless activities that eat up time and resources.<br /><br />The activity trap is the mistake of believing that endless activity is synonomous with results. Nothing could be further from the truth!<br /><br />Think for a moment about people you know. Some of them seem to be always busy but the results from their work are, well, meager. Others, may or may not seem busy but the results of their work are significant.<br /><br />ACTIVITY TRAPS are prized tools of incompetent managers \u2013 to foster their own job security. They shift goalposts to suit their agenda . 95% of the managers belong to this group. They do only things which gets measures and leave a good trail for personal faayada.<br /><br />This CUNT will attack the symptom and not tackle the problem. His derailed mind mistakes his own meaningless activity for achievement.<br /><br />They are endlessly involved in selfish personal brand building<br /><br />They can fool outsiders who see the activity but insiders have a hard time figuring out what they really produce.<br /><br />WHEN YOU ENTER ANY OFFICE YOU CAN SEE PEOPLE IN THE HALL PEERING INTO COMPUTERS-HOW MANY OF THEM ARE DOING REAL WORK<br /><br /><span style=\"color: red;\">http://ajitvadakayil.blogspot.in/2010/12/personal-branding-me-inc-capt-ajit.html</span><br /><br />In reality, uncontrolled activity is a trap and a gigantic source of insecurity. If you are continually consumed by a litany of routine activities, you are actually exposing yourself to obsolescence.<br /><br />Activity traps can lull us into a state of complacency and cause us to lose sight of our visions for the future<br /><br />Unless you know what activity traps who are mired in , you cannot build a firewall , to prevent it from taking over your work life<br /><br />Sometimes the people around you will want to make their urgent priority your priority too. If you allow this to happen it will eat into your finite reserve of time and resources..<br /><br />It\u2019s difficult to manage your time when you constantly fall into the activity trap of responding to other peoples\u2019 demands.. Don\u2019t allow other peoples\u2019 lack of time management affect yours.<br /><br />CONTINUED TO 2-</div>\n</div>\n<div class=\"comment-replies\" id=\"bc_0_21BR\" style=\"background-color: #cccccc; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, Times, FreeSerif, serif; font-size: 16px; margin-left: 36px; margin-top: 1em;\">\n<span id=\"bc_0_21b+seedHPED\" kind=\"d\"><div class=\"comment-thread inline-thread\" id=\"bc_0_20T\" kind=\"t\" style=\"background-color: #eeeeee; margin: 8px 0px; padding: 0.5em 1em;\" t=\"0\" u=\"0\">\n<span class=\"thread-toggle thread-expanded\" id=\"bc_0_20TT\" kind=\"g\" style=\"cursor: pointer; display: inline-block;\"><span class=\"thread-count\" id=\"bc_0_20TN\"><div class=\"thread-dropContainer thread-expanded\" id=\"bc_0_20TD\">\n<span class=\"thread-drop\"></span></div>\n</span></span><ol class=\"thread-chrome thread-expanded\" id=\"bc_0_20TC\" style=\"list-style-type: none; padding: 0px;\">\n<li class=\"comment\" id=\"bc_0_20B\" kind=\"b\" style=\"border-bottom: 0px; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 16px 0px 0px;\"><div class=\"avatar-image-container\" style=\"float: left; margin: 0.2em 0px 0px; max-height: 36px; overflow: hidden; width: 36px;\">\n<img src=\"https://2.bp.blogspot.com/-57G2xiZ-5tM/WJwrrVpmOmI/AAAAAAABQqo/-9wsspdm4RAiWSVRYXpBpkgoVBQdEyLRQCK4B/s35/*\" style=\"border: 1px solid rgb(238, 238, 238); max-width: 36px;\" /></div>\n<div class=\"comment-block\" id=\"c3105669798586344896\" style=\"margin-left: 48px; position: relative;\">\n<div class=\"comment-header\" id=\"bc_0_20M\" kind=\"m\" style=\"margin: 0px 0px 8px;\">\n<cite class=\"user blog-author\" style=\"font-style: normal; font-weight: bold;\"><a href=\"https://www.blogger.com/profile/14410812789424637654\" rel=\"nofollow\" style=\"color: #888888; text-decoration-line: none;\">Capt. Ajit Vadakayil</a></cite><span class=\"icon user blog-author\" style=\"background-image: url(&quot;data:image/png; background-repeat: no-repeat; display: inline-block; font-weight: bold; height: 18px; margin: 0px 0px -4px 6px; width: 18px;\"></span><span class=\"datetime secondary-text\" style=\"margin-left: 6px;\"><a href=\"https://ajitvadakayil.blogspot.com/2009/07/real-work-and-activity-traps-capt-ajit.html?showComment=1512359245254#c3105669798586344896\" rel=\"nofollow\" style=\"color: #888888; text-decoration-line: none;\">December 4, 2017 at 9:17 AM</a></span></div>\n<div class=\"comment-content\" id=\"bc_0_20MC\" style=\"margin-bottom: 8px; text-align: justify;\">\nYou have to manage your activities and not let them manage you. You need to be alert and vigilant as you take control of your own personal activity trap. Activity traps are ways of working that do not enable us to get the best from ourselves.<br /><br />When you are unable to prioritize your workload in a logical way, so that important tasks are completed you fall into activity traps. If you plan does not work, change the plan not your goal.<br /><br />People who get caught in the CHAKRAVYUH of activity traps get BURNT OUT. These people do NOT know the meaning of an exhilarating VICTORY LAP .<br /><br /><span style=\"color: red;\">http://ajitvadakayil.blogspot.in/2010/12/burned-out-versus-stressed-out-capt.html</span><br /><br />How I love to take a victory lap in a hostile stadium<br /><br />IT IS IMPORTANT TO KNOW IF YOUR ARE COMING OR GOING WHITHOUT OPENING YOUR TIFFIN BOX<br /><br />I make a critical statement here \u2013 IF CAPT AJIT VADAKAYIL HAD COMMANDED THE KARGIL WAR , I WOULD HAVE TAKEN ONLY 1% OF THE CASUALITY WE TOOK. I DON\u2019T CARE FOR \u201cYEH DIL MAANGE MORE\u201d WHILE ATTACKING SOME ROCK HILLOCK.<br /><br />I ONCE DEMANDED A SYSTEM CHANGE IN MY SHORE OFFICE. I SAID\u2014 DECLARE WEDNESDAYS FREE OF EMAILS \u2013LET CRITICAL MESSAGES COME FROM SHIP BY FAX .<br /><br />I RIDICULED , WE HAVE DEMENTED MONKEYS IN THE OFFICE WHO SIT BETWEEN A TELEX MACHINE AND A FAX MACHINE ( OF OLDEN TIMES ) , LOOKING ENDLESSLY FROM GANGA BAJOO TO JAMUNA BAJOOO PRETENDING TO BE WORKING HARD.<br /><br />I ASKED- CAN YOU LOAD AND UNLOAD CARGO THIS WAY? SHAOLIN TEMPLE KUNGFU&nbsp;- URUMI SWORD- SWASTIKA TEA LEAF READING CUPS</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;\">this time when i was on leave, &nbsp;i used to watch a programme on HISTORY CHANNEL.</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;\">it was about 2 professional american fighters, going to all corners of the world to learn a martial art , say for 2 weeks. then one of them&nbsp;will challenge the top most fighter of that strain ( karate/ kungfu/ judo etc ).</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TOxTOoSdR3I/AAAAAAAAApI/EKVuHZrQPxc/s1600/1721.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TOxTOoSdR3I/AAAAAAAAApI/EKVuHZrQPxc/s320/1721.jpg\" height=\"217\" width=\"320\" /></span></a></div>\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;\">nobody knows the reason for an elaborate tea drinking ritual \u2013 even today in japan etc.</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;\">japanese call bodhi dharma -- daruma. &nbsp;</span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TQ2Gg_MJbXI/AAAAAAAACFM/DSBPC88UTro/s1600/images+%25286%2529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TQ2Gg_MJbXI/AAAAAAAACFM/DSBPC88UTro/s640/images+%25286%2529.jpg\" height=\"640\" width=\"406\" /></a></div>\n<span class=\"artcopy\" style=\"font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"artcopy\" style=\"font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;\">a tea ceremony is an aesthetic way of entertaining guests, in which everything is done according to an established order. &nbsp;</span><br />\n<span class=\"artcopy\" style=\"font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;\"><span class=\"artcopy\">the&nbsp;</span><span class=\"Apple-style-span\">tea ceremony emphasized the following four qualities: harmony between the guests and the implements used; respect, not only among the participants but also for the utensils; cleanliness, derived from Shint\u014d practices and requiring participants to wash their hands and rinse their mouths as symbolic gestures of cleansing before entering the <i>cha-shitsu;</i> and tranquillity, which is imparted through long and caring use of each article of the tea ceremony.</span></span><br />\n<br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;\"><span style=\"color: blue;\">TEA LEAF READERS- - NEXT TIME READ IN A TEA BOWL WITH SWASTIKA PLACED AT THE BOTTOM.</span></span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;\"><br />\n<span style=\"color: blue;\"> </span></span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"background-color: yellow; font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;\">AND BY THE WAY, IF THE BRITISH HAD TRADED OPIUM FOR COFFEE WITH CHINA INSTEAD OF TEA -- &nbsp;BRITAIN WOULD HAVE BEEN A COFFEE DRINKING NATION.</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"background-color: yellow; font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: 'Times New Roman', serif; line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"color: blue; font-size: large;\"><i>It is a LIE that the\nBritish introduced tea to India. We in Kerala have been growing tea ( chaya ) on\nthe Wayanad Western Ghats since antiquity.&nbsp;&nbsp;</i></span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: 'Times New Roman', serif;
